I Do as far as in me lyeth, License and Authorise the Imprinting of this Book, Intituled, A Second Book of Judgements. To Aprilis 1674. JO. VAUGHAN.
A SECOND BOOK OF Judgements. In Real, Personal, and Mixt Actions, and upon the STATUTE; All or most of them affirmed upon Writs of Error. BEING, The COLLECTION of George Huxley, of Lincolns-Inne Gent. out of the choice Manuscripts of Mr. Brownlowe, and Mr. Moyle, sometimes Protho∣notaries of the COMMON-PLEAS; As also of Mr. Smythier, formerly Secondary of the same Court. Perused, Transcribed, and somewhat Corrected, and Tabled, with Addition of some Notes, by George Townesend Esq Second Prothonotary of the Common Pleas. Very Useful and Necessary for all Prothonotaries, Secondaries, Stu∣dents, Clerks of JUDGEMENTS, and all sorts of Persons any way relating to the Law. Multum in Parvo. LONDON, Printed by T. R. and N. T. for George Dawes over against Lincolns-Inne-Gate in Chancery Lane, 1674.
To the READER. A Book of JUDGEMENTS, (out of which this was tran∣scribed) coming to the hands of a Stationer, who desired to have it Printed if it might be thought fitting; He requested my Perusal thereof, and furtherance therein: I found the same to be most of Special Judgements, or Entries in the Court of Common Pleas, in the times of King JAMES, Queen ELIZABETH, and some Ancienter, for the most part ill written, with too many Abbreviations by &c. without Order, Ta∣ble, or fitting Marginal Notes. Yet finding most part to be of good Matter and Forms, and thinking it fit to be Pub∣lished:
I first Tabled it, and then caused it to be written forth in as good a Method as I could; which I Perused, and some∣what Corrected, adding Marginal Notes. I conceive the same principally to concern the Prothonotaries of the Court of Com∣mon Pleas, and their Clerks of Judge∣ments, but may be often useful to Clerks of the Kings Bench, the Exchequer, Ireland, Counties Palatine, Franchises, and Corporarions, and many other Practi∣cers at Law. Publick Charity more than any my own Profit, concerns, or Interest, incited me to this work, which, if well ac∣cepted, I have my ends. I stile this A Se∣cond Book of Judgements, there being a former Book of Judgements in English, Published in the Year, 1655. Primo Aprilis 1674. GEORGE TOWNESEND.
